Solace Square

    Solace Square is a large clearing that is surrounded on all sides by
huge vallenwood trees. These trees stretch far above the ground and their
limbs provide cover and shelter to the inhabitants of Solace. The clearing
here rises slightly towards the center of the square, providing a high spot
in the center. Small roads have been cut into the dense forest to the
north, south, east, and west. On one edge of the square, there is a huge
vallenwood which bough supports a collection of huts and buildings. A
small spiral staircase leads up around the trunk of the tree and into the
thick limbs which house the buildings.
A long torch functions as a street lamp here.

Court of the Aghar
    This is the throne room created for the Highbulp of the gully dwarves
who reside in Xak Tsaroth. Large swaths of garish golden and silver cloth
have been draped throughout the room, wrapped haphazardly around and
between columns, creating a mind-boggling array of shimmering decor. Hung
over the excessive amounts of metallic cloth are a large number of ancient
tapestries that were once probably quite beautiful but have since been
'improved' upon by the gully dwarves with brightly colored paint, creating
an even more confusing and blinding display of interior design. As though
that itself were not enough, a number of graceful nude statues adorn the
room, also 'improved' by the gully dwarves with an almost disturbing amount
of realism and detail. At the head of the room sits a large ornamental
throne decorated with the finest objects of an even remotely shiny fashion
that could be found.

Court of the Aghar

    This is the throne room created for the Highbulp of the gully dwarves
who reside in Xak Tsaroth. Large swaths of garish golden and silver cloth
have been draped throughout the room, wrapped haphazardly around and
between columns, creating a mind-boggling array of shimmering decor. Hung
over the excessive amounts of metallic cloth are a large number of ancient
tapestries that were once probably quite beautiful but have since been
'improved' upon by the gully dwarves with brightly colored paint, creating
an even more confusing and blinding display of interior design. As though
that itself were not enough, a number of graceful nude statues adorn the
room, also 'improved' by the gully dwarves with an almost disturbing amount
of realism and detail. At the head of the room sits a large ornamental
throne decorated with the finest objects of an even remotely shiny fashion
that could be found.
A small vial of milky liquid has carelessly been left here.
A small roll of bread lies here. [3]
a shirt made of black silk lies here.
A pair of silky pants lies here.
A pair of fingerless silk gloves lie here.
A pair of loose silk sleeves has been left here.
A long, hooded cloak has been left here.
A simple looking wooden club is here.
A small roll of bread lies here. [8]
The corpse of Yvlylxly is lying here.
A shimmering portal casts a blue light on the area...it glows dimly
Dressed in colorful rags Bupu stands next to the throne of the Highbulp.

he spe de po


Spell    : Deep pockets

Sphere   : Enchantment
Usage    : cast 'deep pockets' [cloth or leather container  in inventory]
Duration : Permanent
Effects  : Makes a container grow in size

By casting this spell on a cloth or leather garment, the caster makes the item
grow in size by adding dimensional pockets in the item.  The pockets are
small, dimensional pockets that form inside the object and link to another
plane of existence beyond the prime material plane.  Objects can then be
stored in the dimensional pockets, giving the object more space.

Because of the nature of dimensional rifts, this spell will eventually eat
away at the material of the item until the entire item becomes a part of the
plane the pockets were created from.

Details:
- Makes a cloth or leather container larger, but reduces its useful life.

Component Casting:
-Increased size bonus beyond the normal cap.

golden double doors, identical to the pair you can see beyond the statue of
Mishakal to the west.
